<review>Fantastic spot that many people don't know about when visiting Pebble Beach. You have to time the tides or access will be under water. If you know where to go, you can cut through the golf course and the a set of stairs down. Plenty of errant golf balls to pick up and the views are incredible on a sunny day. I'm not sure if you can access the beach without a resident badge or if you can pay to get in, but it's worth it.< /review>< pictures>

< review>
As someone who is a serious chocolaholic, I'm always on the lookout for the best chocolate drinks or desserts. I think Starbuck's Mocha Frapp is pretty good, esp. if you request an additional pump (or half pump) of mocha (chocolate) And Peet's has a Mocha Javiva which can be good and isn't too coffee-strong. But then I discovered Willy's Mocha Mania. It's a sensational smoothie that uses nonfat yogurt (that I can't taste), chocolate, coffee and whatever secret ingredients it has. The manager told me that it's been around for 20 years. No surprise. I also like Willy's version of a Creamsicle (orange/vanilla smoothie) but for chocolaholics the Mocha Mania is IT. The staff are very friendly at the place, helped no doubt by my being a familiar customer with a serious Mocha Mania addiction. They're very sympathetic to that.<//review>

<UserId.>108204136824597170531< /UserId.><name>Lisa Tuholski</name><Date>1564258225009<//Date><rating>5< /rating><review>Came on a lazy Saturday afternoon for the first time and found friendly baristas, good coffee, and a breakfast sandwich that exceeded expectations...mostly because it only cost $9 and came with salad and fresh fruit! Most places in LA will happily charge you $9 for a sandwich and extra for anything fresh or green. Croissant was super flaky and fresh as well.

Additional bonus: it has the vibe of a coffee shop but also serves good hot food. A lot of places will pop up on Google/Yelp as "coffee shops" but they're really diners; or they're a coffee shop with some pastries and pre made sandwiches in a case at the front. Nothing wrong with either of those kinds of places, but I love a coffee shop that also serves good made to order food.

Order at the counter and they'll bring food out to you. Indoor & outdoor seating options. Likely gets busy during the week but very chill around noon on a Saturday. Will definitely be back the next time I'm in Pico Robertson!</review>< pics>

Elk Grove Pediatrics is NOT the same quality doctors office it once was. The support staff has completely changed. After a rather large mix-up in regards to a vaccine given to my daughter in October, and confusion as to which one was due because her record showed she had been given flu shot, which she happens to be allergic to, I have less than favorable opinion in regards to not only their organizational skills, but mostly their LACK of professionalism.  When nurse assistant called to let me know the mix up was straightened out and not to worry, I asked that her supervisor called and requested the documentation to reflect the corrected mistake. I was told no I could not have a copy of paperwork, and no one, not nurse or more importantly the doctor whom my daughter has seen since she was 5, qnow 14, didn't even have the kindness to call me to apologize or reassure me this mistake was simply a clerical error. I had truly thought she was a good doctor, who really had me fooled, as I thought lal these years she cared. Clearly the office has a total lack of organization, as well as complete lack of professionalism. This office is not a good doctors office for children, and families.
I only gave star so it allowed me to post.
